## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of a chemical species concentration (dA/dt) as a function of time and current concentration. In chemical kinetics, rate laws typically express dA/dt as functions of concentration A, with possible time dependence for non-autonomous systems (e.g., photochemical reactions, periodic forcing).

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order decay: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A (rate proportional to concentration)
- Second-order reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (rate proportional to square of concentration)
- nth-order reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (first-order with equilibrium offset)
- Mixed order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (competing first and second order)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (saturation kinetics)
- Autocatalytic reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (logistic-type growth/decay)
- Inhibition kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A**2) (substrate inhibition)
- Consecutive reaction: dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) + c2 * A (time-dependent source with first-order decay)
- Fractional order with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (fractional order with constant production)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (Hill-type equation)
- Time-modulated rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (time-dependent rate constant)
- Second-order reversible: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 + c1 * A + c2 (quadratic polynomial in A)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative proportionality to concentration тЖТ first-order irreversible decay: dA_dt = -k*A
- Rate law with integer power of concentration тЖТ elementary reaction step with molecularity equal to the power
- Concentration appearing in both numerator and denominator тЖТ enzyme/saturation kinetics (Michaelis-Menten mechanism)
- Product of concentration and (constant minus concentration) тЖТ autocatalytic or logistic kinetics indicating a species that both catalyzes and is consumed
- Constant term plus concentration-dependent term тЖТ reversible reaction approaching equilibrium or constant production/influx
- Quadratic dependence on A with negative leading coefficient тЖТ second-order decay or dimerization reaction
- Explicit time dependence in rate expression тЖТ non-autonomous system such as photolysis with varying light intensity or sequential reaction intermediates
- Sum of exponential terms in time тЖТ superposition of parallel reaction pathways with different rate constants
